### Summary: Include screen shots or a video of your app highlighting its features

### Focus Areas: What specific areas of the project did you prioritize? Why did you choose to focus on these areas?
Lots of time spent on unit tests, from my experience proper test coverage saves 10x time in future, when we don't have to deal with wierd 

### Time Spent: Approximately how long did you spend working on this project? How did you allocate your time?
basic project struct setup      20 min
Swiftlint setup                 5 min 
git setup                       5 min
Network layer                   30 min 
Unit Tests for network layer    1.5 hours 
UI Layer style development 
ViewModel

### Weakest Part of the Project: What do you think is the weakest part of your project?

                                                                                                                                <p>Make this seasonal apple and blackberry crumble for a comforting family pud. Pre-cooking the topping will make it extra-crispy,

                                                                                                                                                    <div class="recipe__instructions" data-placement="RecipeInstructions">
                                                                                                                                                        <div class="tabbed-list" data-component="TabbedList">
                                                                                                                                                            <div class="tabbed-list__header">
                                                                                                                                                                <h2 class="tabbed-list__tab heading-3"><button type="button" class="tabbed-list__tab-button tabbed-list__tab-button--active" data-feature="TabbedListButton" data-feature-variant="Left" data-index="1">Ingredients</button></h2>
                                                                                                                                                                <h2 class="tabbed-list__tab heading-3"><button type="button" class="tabbed-list__tab-button" data-feature="TabbedListButton" data-feature-variant="Right" data-index="2">Nutrition</button></h2></div>
                                                                                                                                                            <div class="tabbed-list__content">
                                                                                                                                                                <div class="">
                                                                                                                                                                    <section id="ingredients-list" class="ingredients-list" data-component="IngredientsList" data-feature="Recipe Instructions"
                                                                                                                                                                    data-stitcher-dai-container="ingredients-list">
                                                                                                                                                                        <section>
                                                                                                                                                                            <h3 class="ingredients-list__heading mb-sm heading-5">For the crumble topping</h3>
                                                                                                                                                                            <ul class="ingredients-list list">
                                                                                                                                                                                <li class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">120g <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/flour-glossary" data-component="Link">plain flour</a></li>
                                                                                                                                                                                <li
                                                                                                                                                                                class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">60g <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/sugar-glossary" data-component="Link">caster sugar</a></li>
                                                                                                                                                                                    <li
                                                                                                                                                                                    class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top list-item--separator-bottom">60g <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/butter-glossary" data-component="Link">unsalted butter</a>
                                                                                                                                                                                        <div
                                                                                                                                                                                        class="ingredients-list__item-note"> at room temperature, cut into pieces</div>
                                                                                                                                                                </li>
                                                                                                                                                                </ul>
                                                                                                                                                                </section>
                                                                                                                                                                <section>
                                                                                                                                                                    <h3 class="ingredients-list__heading mb-sm mt-sm heading-5">For the fruit compote</h3>
                                                                                                                                                                    <ul class="ingredients-list list">
                                                                                                                                                                        <li class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">300g <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/apple-glossary" data-component="Link">Braeburn apple</a></li>
                                                                                                                                                                        <li
                                                                                                                                                                        class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">30g <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/butter-glossary" data-component="Link">unsalted butter</a></li>
                                                                                                                                                                            <li
                                                                                                                                                                            class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">30g <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/sugar-glossary" data-component="Link">demerara sugar</a></li>
                                                                                                                                                                                <li
                                                                                                                                                                                class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">115g <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/blackberry-glossary" data-component="Link">blackberries</a></li>
                                                                                                                                                                                    <li
                                                                                                                                                                                    class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top"><a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/cinnamon-glossary" data-component="Link">¼ tsp ground cinnamon</a></li>
                                                                                                                                                                                        <li
                                                                                                                                                                                        class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top"><a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/vanilla-glossary" data-component="Link">vanilla</a>
                                                                                                                                                                                            <div
                                                                                                                                                                                            class="ingredients-list__item-note"> ice cream, to serve</div>
                                                                                                                                                            </li>
                                                                                                                                                            </ul>
                                                                                                                                                            </section>
                                                                                                                                                            </section>
                                                                                                                                                        </div>
                                                                                                                                                        <div class="d-none">
                                                                                                                                                            <p class="recipe__nutritions-caption">Nutrition: per serving</p>
                                                                                                                                                            <ul class="nutrition-list">
                                                                                                                                                                <li class="nutrition-list__item"><span class="fw-600 mr-1">kcal</span>409</li>
                                                                                                                                                                <li class="nutrition-list__item"><span class="fw-600 mr-1">fat</span>19
                                                                                                                                                                    <!-- -->g</li>

                                                                                                                                                                    <!-- -->g</li>

                                                                                                                                                                    <!-- -->g</li>

                                                                                                                                                                    <!-- -->g</li>

                                                                                                                                                                    <!-- -->g</li>

                                                                                                                                                                    <!-- -->g</li>

                                                                                                                                                                    <!-- -->g
                                                                                                                                                                    <div class="nutrition-list__additional-text">low
                                                                                                                                                                        <div class="nutrition-list__additional-text-icon"><i class="icon" style="width:12px;min-width:12px;height:12px;min-height:12px;animation-duration:1000ms;transform:rotate(180deg)"><svg class="icon__svg" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" style="color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 1);fill:rgba(255, 255, 255, 1)"><use xlink:href="/static/icons/base/sprite-maps/arrows-71cd4ec91a6536f2abcc71183b8f0de8.svg#arrow-light"></use></svg></i></div>

                                                                                                                                                <div class="ad-slot hidden-print ad-slot__below-ingredients align-items-center">
                                                                                                                                                    <div class="ad-slot__container below-ingredients--1">
                                                                                                                                                        <div id="recipe--below-ingredients--1" class="ad-unit"></div>
                                                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                                                    <div>

                                                                                                                                                            (window.adq = window.adq || []).push((api) => api.addSlot({"key":"below-ingredients","index":1,"searchTerm":null,"fullSearchTerm":null}));
                                                                                                                                                        </script>
                                                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                                                <div class="js-piano-recipe-method col-12 pa-reset">
                                                                                                                                                    <section class="method-steps mb-lg" data-placement="MethodList">
                                                                                                                                                        <h2 class="method-steps__heading heading-3">Method</h2>
                                                                                                                                                        <ul class="method-steps__list">
                                                                                                                                                            <li class="method-steps__list-item">
                                                                                                                                                                <h3 class="method-steps__item-heading heading-5">step 1</h3>
                                                                                                                                                                <div class="editor-content">
                                                                                                                                                                    <p>Heat oven to 190C/170C fan/gas 5. Tip 120g plain flour and 60g caster sugar into a large
                                                                                                                                                                        <a href="/review/best-mixing-bowls" data-id="iframe-1-anchor-0">bowl</a>.</p>
                                                                                                                                                                    <div class="ad-placement"
                                                                                                                                                                    data-count="100"></div>
                                                                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                                                            </li>
                                                                                                                                                            <li class="method-steps__list-item">
                                                                                                                                                                <h3 class="method-steps__item-heading heading-5">step 2</h3>
                                                                                                                                                                <div class="editor-content">
                                                                                                                                                                    <p>Add 60g unsalted butter, then rub into the flour using your fingertips to make a light
                                                                                                                                                                        breadcrumb texture. Do not overwork it or the crumble will become heavy.</p>
                                                                                                                                                                    <div class="ad-placement"
                                                                                                                                                                    data-count="265"></div>
                                                                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                                                            </li>
                                                                                                                                                            <li class="method-steps__list-item">
                                                                                                                                                                <h3 class="method-steps__item-heading heading-5">step 3</h3>
                                                                                                                                                                <div class="editor-content">
                                                                                                                                                                    <p>Sprinkle the mixture evenly over a <a href="/review/best-baking-trays" data-id="iframe-3-anchor-0">baking sheet</a>                                                                                                                                                                        and bake for 15 mins or until lightly coloured.</p>
                                                                                                                                                                    <div class="ad-placement" data-count="366"></div>
                                                                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                                                            </li>
                                                                                                                                                            <li class="method-steps__list-item">
                                                                                                                                                                <h3 class="method-steps__item-heading heading-5">step 4</h3>
                                                                                                                                                                <div class="editor-content">
                                                                                                                                                                    <p>Meanwhile, for the compote, <a href="/review/test-five-best-peelers" data-id="iframe-4-anchor-0">peel</a>,
                                                                                                                                                                        core and cut 300g Braeburn apples into 2cm dice.</p>
                                                                                                                                                                    <div class="ad-placement" data-count="454"></div>
                                                                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                                                            </li>
                                                                                                                                                            <li class="method-steps__list-item">
                                                                                                                                                                <h3 class="method-steps__item-heading heading-5">step 5</h3>
                                                                                                                                                                <div class="editor-content">
                                                                                                                                                                    <p>Put 30g unsalted butter and 30g demerara sugar in a medium <a href="/review/five-best-saucepans"
                                                                                                                                                                        data-id="iframe-5-anchor-0">saucepan</a> and melt together over a medium heat. Cook
                                                                                                                                                                        for 3 mins until the mixture turns to a light caramel.</p>
                                                                                                                                                                    <div class="ad-placement"
                                                                                                                                                                    data-count="625"></div>
                                                                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                                                            </li>
                                                                                                                                                            <li class="method-steps__list-item">
                                                                                                                                                                <h3 class="method-steps__item-heading heading-5">step 6</h3>
                                                                                                                                                                <div class="editor-content">
                                                                                                                                                                    <p>Stir in the apples and cook for 3 mins. Add 115g blackberries and ¼ tsp ground cinnamon,
                                                                                                                                                                        and cook for 3 mins more.</p>
                                                                                                                                                                    <div class="ad-placement" data-count="745"></div>
                                                                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                                                            </li>
                                                                                                                                                            <li class="method-steps__list-item">
                                                                                                                                                                <h3 class="method-steps__item-heading heading-5">step 7</h3>
                                                                                                                                                                <div class="editor-content">
                                                                                                                                                                    <p>Cover, remove from the heat, then leave for 2-3 mins to continue cooking in the warmth
                                                                                                                                                                        of the pan.</p>
                                                                                                                                                                    <div class="ad-placement" data-count="849"></div>
                                                                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                                                            </li>
                                                                                                                                                            <li class="method-steps__list-item">
                                                                                                                                                                <h3 class="method-steps__item-heading heading-5">step 8</h3>
                                                                                                                                                                <div class="editor-content">
                                                                                                                                                                    <p>To serve, spoon the warm fruit into an ovenproof gratin dish, top with the crumble mix,
                                                                                                                                                                        then reheat in the oven for 5-10 mins. Serve with vanilla ice cream.</p>
                                                                                                                                                                    <div class="ad-placement"
                                                                                                                                                                    data-count="1011"></div>
                                                                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                                                            </li>
                                                                                                                                                        </ul>
                                                                                                                                                    </section>
                                                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                                            </div>
                                                                                                                                        </div>
                                                                                                                                    </div>
